Now, verse 21 is one of the definitive verses in the Bible on the inspiration of the Scriptures. Second Timothy 3:16 may tell you that ["all scripture is given by inspiration of God,"]{.class_s35R} but 2 Peter 1:21 tells you how it's done.

["For the prophecy came not in old time by the will of men."]{.class_s35R} The standard charge of all infidels against the Bible is that it's just a book written by men. But nobody in the Old Testament decided of his own will that he was going to sit down and write Scripture or stand up and speak the word of the Lord. You take a man like Jonah: he didn't even want to preach to Nineveh. Amos said, ["I was no prophet, neither was I a prophet's son; but I was an herdman, and a gatherer of sycamore fruit: and the ]{.class_s35R}[Lord ]{.class_s35X-0}[took me as I followed the flock, and the ]{.class_s35R}[Lord ]{.class_s35X-0}[said unto me, Go, prophecy:]{.class_s35R} (Amos 7:14--15).

Jeremiah resigned from the ministry. Jeremiah 20:9, ["Then I said, I WILL NOT make mention of him, nor speak anymore in his name. But his word was in mine heart as a burning fire\...and I was weary with forbearing, and I could not stay."]{.class_s35R}

[Not even Moses wanted to speak God's words]{.class_s35S} (Exod. 3--4)! If the writing of the Scriptures had been left up to its human authors, you would have no Bible today.

["But holy men of God."]{.class_s35R} Isn't it amazing how the Lord overlooks the sins of the saints in the New Testament? Those ["holy men"]{.class_s35R} were men like [Moses ]{.class_s35S}who murdered a man, []{#c2NP.xhtml_page_441}[Joshua ]{.class_s35S}who failed to pray about Ai and the men of Gibeon, [David ]{.class_s35S}who committed adultery and murder, and [Daniel ]{.class_s35S}who let a king bow down and offer sacrifices to him.

In the Old Testament, God [records ]{.class_s35S}those sins and He [punishes ]{.class_s35S}those sins and He forgives those sins, but when you get to the New Testament, the blood of Jesus Christ [took away ]{.class_s35S}those sins and allowed the Lord to take those saints from Abraham's Bosom to Heaven (Eph. 4:8).

So when the New Testament talks about those Old Testament saints, it either ignores the sin altogether or, if the character is being used as an example for your admonition as Lot is used in 2 Peter 2:7--8, it actually [emphasizes ]{.class_s35S}his righteousness and [down ]{.class_s35S}plays his sin.

Now, those ["holy men"]{.class_s35R} were sinners just like we are, but in the Old Testament, their lives were characterized by their righteous living. Where they did commit heinous sins (like David), they repented, and the Lord did not impute that sin to them (Rom. 4:6--8).

They were also ["holy"]{.class_s35R} in the sense that God had set them apart to give out His words. You take someone like Jeremiah; he was chosen to be a prophet before he was even born (Jer. 1:5).

Back in verse 21; notice [how]{.class_s35S} the Scriptures were [originally]{.class_s35S} given. ["But holy men of God SPAKE as they were moved by the Holy Ghost."]{.class_s35R} So when Paul says, ["All scripture is given by inspiration,"]{.class_s35R} the giving actually had nothing to do with the [writing]{.class_s35S} at all.

All of this emphasis on the "original text" and the "original autographs" is nothing but a bunch of baloney. The word [inspiration]{.class_s35S} means "God-breathed," and God breathed through the [mouths]{.class_s35S} of His prophets when they [spake. That's when]{.class_s35S} the inspiration [occurred]{.class_s35S}, not when it was [written]{.class_s35S}.

If you want a clear example of how it was done, the Lord gives you one in Jeremiah 36. There, the word of the Lord []{#c2NP.xhtml_page_442}["came unto Jeremiah:]{.class_s35R} (Jer. 36:1). So the inspiration took place with Jeremiah. But did Jeremiah write anything down on paper? [Not on your life, brother.]{.class_s35S}

Jeremiah 36:4, ["Then Jeremiah called Baruch the son of Neriah: AND BARUCH WROTE FROM THE MOUTH OF JEREMIAH all the words of the ]{.class_s35R}[Lord]{.class_s35X-0}[, which he had spoken unto him."]{.class_s35R}

So this business about [only ]{.class_s35S}the "original autographs at the hand of the apostles and prophets" being inspired is a Biblical [heresy. ]{.class_s35S}Second Peter 1:21 says they were written at [the mouth ]{.class_s35S}of someone who was [speaking]{.class_s35S} by inspiration. That is why the highly accurate, scientific [King James Version]{.class_s35S} says, ["all scripture is GIVEN by inspiration."]{.class_s35R} That is the [historically accurate account]{.class_s35S}. The reading of the modern versions ([RSV, NASV, NIV,]{.class_s35S} etc.), "All scripture is inspired by God," is not what 2 Peter 1:21 says. The apostates who keep saying that will take 36,000 ([RSV, NASV]{.class_s35S}) to 64,000 ([NIV]{.class_s35S}) words out of your Bible and still claim to be orthodox because he believes "all scripture is inspired by God."

Ahh, go blow it out your nose.

We're Bible-believers, man. We believe 2 Peter 1:21 says God [gave]{.class_s35S} ["holy men of God"]{.class_s35R} the words to speak. Those words were written down and preserved for us, and God gave us those words in English in a [King James, Authorized Version,]{.class_s35S} originally published in 1611.

Genesis 2:7 and Ezekiel 37 shows you how God "inspired" the WRITINGS[ after]{.class_s35S} they were written if no speaker spoke them.

You say, "What about all the people in foreign lands that don't speak English, and what about all the people before 1611?"

Well, the Lord may have done something different for them, but that's not really your problem, is it? You don't care one whit about the people who have the [Valera ]{.class_s35S}version (Spanish) or []{#c2NP.xhtml_page_443}the [Diodati ]{.class_s35S}version (Italian) or the [Olivetan]{.class_s35S}, [Martin]{.class_s35S}, or [Segond ]{.class_s35S}versions (French) or the [Synodal ]{.class_s35S}version (Russian) or those who had the [Wycliffe Bible]{.class_s35S} or [Tyndale's New Testament]{.class_s35S} or [Roger's Bible]{.class_s35S} or the [Great Bible]{.class_s35S} or the [Bishops' Bible]{.class_s35S} or the [Geneva Bible]{.class_s35S}. [Your problem is with the Bible GOD GAVE YOU. ]{.class_s35S}You don't like it and can't stand it and won't leave it alone because it knows all about you and tells it.

You're like B. F. Westcott and Fenton J. Hort. To you that Book is "vile." That's why they changed it; that's why the scholars have been changing it ever since. And don't tell me that's not how you feel about the matter. If you didn't think it was [dirty]{.class_s35S}, you wouldn't be trying to "clean it up," would you?

That's not how I, or the people that follow me, look at the Book at all. I think that [AV 1611 ]{.class_s35S}is a [holy]{.class_s35S} Book (vs. 21) that is [sure]{.class_s35S} (vs. 19) and [precious]{.class_s35S} (vs. 4). That's why we leave it alone. We let [it]{.class_s35S} clean [us]{.class_s35S} up. Our sentiments are summed up on one verse.

Psalm 119:140, ["Thy word is VERY PURE: therefore thy servant LOVETH IT."]{.class_s35R}

That's ["love it," ]{.class_s35S}not ["change it."]{.class_s35S}

[]{#c2W0.xhtml}

## Chapter 2 {.heading_s3A-0}

2:1 But there were false prophets also among the people, even as there shall be false teachers among you, who privily shall bring in damnable heresies, even denying the Lord that bought them, and bring upon themselves swift destruction.

2 And many shall follow their pernicious ways; by reason of whom the way of truth shall be evil spoken of.

3 And through covetousness shall they with feigned words make merchandise of you: whose judgment now of a long time lingereth not, and their damnation slumbereth not.

In chapter 2 there are two classes of people discussed throughout the chapter. Those two classes are given in verse 1; they are ["false prophets"]{.class_s35R} and ["false teachers."]{.class_s35R} And when you get down to verse 22, those two classes are identified by gender. The false prophets are [male]{.class_s35S}, and the false teachers are [female]{.class_s35S}.

Look at 2 Peter 2:22. ["But it is happened unto THEM."]{.class_s35R} The ["them"]{.class_s35R} are the false prophets and false teachers discussed throughout the chapter. ["The dog is turned to HIS own vomit."]{.class_s35R} In respect to verse one, that is the false prophets; they're men. ["The sow that was washed to HER wallowing in the mire."]{.class_s35R} Respectively, the "sow" is the false teachers; they're women.

Now, we were on pretty firm ground in 2 Peter chapter 1. In chapter 1, there was little, if any, doctrinal application outside of the Church Age. But starting with chapter 2, things start to change.

[Historically]{.class_s35S}, Peter is making a comparison between the false prophets that troubled the people of Israel in the Old Testament and false teachers that would trouble the churches. And while []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_445}there is enough of a problem with false women teachers in the Church Age (Ellen G. White and Mary Baker Eddy, for example) that Paul has to warn against it (1 Tim. 2:12), most of the false teachers in the book of Acts and the Pauline epistles were [men ]{.class_s35S}(e.g., Acts 15:1).

But in the Tribulation, you have a different situation. The false prophets return (Matt. 24:11). Also in the Tribulation, you have [women ]{.class_s35S}teaching idolatry connected with adultery and fornication (vss. 14, 22 cf. Rev. 2:20 and comments in that Commentary).

So though you may run into some pre-Tribulation references such as verses 5 and 8, most of the doctrinal application will be [Tribulational]{.class_s35S}.

Also notice, before going further, how closely this chapter parallels the book of Jude. The material is almost identical. Second Peter 2 has references to Noah and Lot that Jude does not include, and Jude gives information on the body of Moses and the preaching of Enoch that is revealed nowhere else in the Scriptures. Other than that, the content is exactly the same. So as we comment on 2 Peter 2, we will not go into the depth we went into in the book of Jude. If you want a more detailed study of the contents of this chapter, I refer you to that Commentary in [The Bible Believer's Commentary on the General Epistles,]{.class_s35S} Volume 2.

Notice in verse 1 that when the false teachers come in that it is ["privily";]{.class_s35R} i.e., privately, [secretly]{.class_s35S}. That is how Westcott and Hort introduced the Alexandrian Greek text into the [RV]{.class_s35S} committee from 1871--1876. They furnished it in installments to the members of the committee [under oath of secrecy]{.class_s35S}, after being instructed by the Convocation of the Anglican Church in Canterbury that a new translation was [not]{.class_s35S} to be made and that as [few changes as possibl]{.class_s35S}e be made to the text of the [Authorized Version. ]{.class_s35S}The result was a new translation based on a new Greek []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_446}text that attacked the Trinity (1 John 5:7), the Deity of Christ (1 Tim. 3:16), the Virgin Birth (Matt. 1:25; Luke 2:33; Acts 4:27, 30), the Blood Atonement (Col. 1:14), the Resurrection of Christ (Acts 1:3), the Ascension of Christ (Luke 24:51--52), etc.

In other words, Westcott and Hort were [false teachers ]{.class_s35S}who privately brought in ["damnable heresies"]{.class_s35R} onto the Bible revision committees of the late 19th, 20th, and 21st centuries; and those ["heresies"]{.class_s35R} were so ["damnable"]{.class_s35R} that most of them denied some aspect of the doctrine of Christ. Modern Bible versions are a direct fulfillment of 2 Peter 2:1.

["Even denying the Lord that bought them."]{.class_s35R} That is a direct slam against the Calvinistic doctrine of limited atonement. The blood atonement of Jesus Christ ["bought"]{.class_s35R} unsaved prophets and teachers who denied and rejected the [payment]{.class_s35S}. So when Christ died on the cross, He [paid the price]{.class_s35S} for the elect [and]{.class_s35S} the non-elect. The fact that these people deny ["the Lord that bought them, and bring upon themselves swift destruction"]{.class_s35R} is not God's doing ("reprobation"); it's theirs.

["And many shall follow their pernicious ways"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 2). ["Pernicious"]{.class_s35R} means [destructive. ]{.class_s35S}Proverbs 14:12 says, ["There is a way which seemeth right unto a man, but the end thereof are the ways of death."]{.class_s35R} Jesus said, ["Broad is the way, that leadeth to destruction, and many there be which go in thereat"]{.class_s35R} (Matt. 7:13).

When the Bible says ["many,"]{.class_s35R} brother; it means it. Between Mohammed and the Pope, [two billion]{.class_s35S} people are being led down the broad way to Hell. Brigham Young and Joseph Smith (Mormons) claim another [eight million,]{.class_s35S} while Charles Russell and Judge Rutherford (Jehovah's Witnesses) lead [twelve million]{.class_s35S} into the Pit.

That's the Church Age---right now. When it comes to the Tribulation, look how many times Jesus emphasized that word []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_447}["many."]{.class_s35R} Matthew 24:5,[ "For MANY shall come in my name, saying, I am Christ; and shall deceive MANY."]{.class_s35R} Verses 10--12 of Matthew 24: ["And then shall MANY be offended\...And MANY false prophets shall rise, and shall deceive MANY. And because iniquity shall abound, the love of MANY shall wax cold."]{.class_s35R}

Those who follow the truth in any age are [minorities]{.class_s35S}. As we are about to see in the following verses of this chapter, it was the [majority ]{.class_s35S}who died in the Flood of Noah's day. God burned the [majority ]{.class_s35S}in Sodom and Gomorrah.

It was the [majority ]{.class_s35S}in Christ's day who had Him crucified. It was the [majority ]{.class_s35S}that drove Paul out of Antioch of Pisidia and stoned him at Lystra.

Are you with the "[majority ]{.class_s35S}of Christian scholars" when it comes to belief in a King James Bible? Then undoubtedly you are in the wrong, for the majority has seldom been right about [anything]{.class_s35S}.

I have always been in a "minority," even during my unsaved days. The vice-principal of my high school used to get up in assemblies and say, "Most of you young people are doing well here; it is only[ two percent]{.class_s35S} that are causing the trouble." The "two percent" was a reference to me and the guys with whom I hung around.

[Socially]{.class_s35S}, I am part of a dwindling minority in the United States. I am a White Anglo-Saxon Protestant (a WASP), and I am a ["straight" male.]{.class_s35S}

[Religiously]{.class_s35S}, I am part of a [staggering minority]{.class_s35S}. I am an independent Baptist who believes the [King James Bible]{.class_s35S} from cover to cover (including the cover) and who won't correct one word of it even where it crosses Baptist theology and tradition.

Now, all of that is pretty narrow, brother. But if I am doing what God told me to do and believing what God told me to believe, what do I care if BJU and Tennessee Temple and BBC []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_448}and PCC and Moody, Wheaton, Fuller, and Dallas Theological Seminary and the UN and the NAACP and the ACLU are all against me? Bob Jones Sr. said, "You and God make a majority." I'm on the winning side, brethren.

Someone told Martin Luther once, "Don't you know the whole world is against you, Martin." And that old Kraut head replied, "[Then I'm against it]{.class_s35S}!"

["By reason of whom the way of truth shall be evil spoken of."]{.class_s35R} It's not enough for them to destroy the people they win; they have to sour the general populace against [you]{.class_s35S}.

We have experienced that here at PBI, during our street preaching. During the great "Brownsville Revival," some of the young men who were being trained at Kilpatrick's "School of Ministry" were  trying to disrupt our Saturday night street meetings in downtown Pensacola.

After claiming to have brought down the crime rate in Pensacola (when it actually [rose]{.class_s35S}---see [Modern Charismatic Revival Doctrines Examined]{.class_s35S}), and after being unable to shut down any bar within [three blocks ]{.class_s35S}of the church, all those Charismatic nuts could find time to do, after retreading nearly a million professing Charismatic "Christians" ([not one in a thousand made a first-time profession of faith)]{.class_s35S}, [was to interfere with a bunch of Bible-believing young men who were actually trying to win lost sinners to Christ.]{.class_s35S}

More recently, some thin-skinned sissy has decided to try to intimidate our young men from preaching downtown. At first he would spit in their faces and knock their Bibles out of their hands. When that didn't work, he resorted to passing out his own handwritten tracts against the street preachers and holding up a sign saying, "I'm with stupid."

We have gotten criticism like that by the Christians of this town for years; that fellow merely decided he would go beyond []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_449}talk. But that's the way [the religious crowd ]{.class_s35S}feels about Biblical street preaching---they speak evil of it.

["And through covetousness shall they with feigned words make merchandise of you"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 3). That's the motive---it's money. It's 1 Timothy 6:5, which has been changed in the new "Bibles." ["Perverse disputings of men of corrupt minds, and destitute of the truth, supposing that gain is godliness."]{.class_s35R} Peter says down in verse 14, ["an heart they have exercised with covetous practices."]{.class_s35R}

["Whose judgment now of a long time lingereth not, and their damnation slumbereth now."]{.class_s35R} That's a reference to the Tribulation, as can be seen by the two examples that follow: the Flood and the destruction of Sodom and Gomorrah. The idea is that God has put off the judgment for long enough, and it is finally going to come.

That's what happened before the Flood. The Lord revealed to Enoch that when his son died, God would send judgment on the world. That's why Enoch named his son Methuselah; the name means "[When he is dead, it shall be sent]{.class_s35S}!" The judgment of God lingered for 969 years, but when Methuselah died,[ it came.]{.class_s35S}

In the case of Sodom and Gomorrah, the Lord had enough "on them" to burn them back in Genesis 13:13, but He waited until their cry had waxed ["great"]{.class_s35R} and their sin was ["very grievous"]{.class_s35R} (Gen. 18:20; 19:13).

Back in Genesis 15:16, the Lord described His judgment like a cup that the Amorites would fill with their sins, and then the Lord would judge them.

4 For if God spared not the angels that sinned, but cast them down to hell, and delivered them into chains of darkness, to be reserved unto judgment;

5 And spared not the old world, but saved Noah the eighth person, a preacher of righteousness, bringing in the flood upon the world of the ungodly;

6 And turning the cities of Sodom and Gomorrha into ashes condemned them with an overthrow, making them an ensample unto those that after should live ungodly;

7 And delivered just Lot, vexed with the filthy conversation of the wicked:

8 (For that righteous man dwelling among them, in seeing and hearing, vexed his righteous soul from day to day with their unlawful deeds;)

Verse 4 is a reference to the sons of God in Genesis 6. Notice that verse 5 is a continuation of what happened in verse 4.

Verse 5 is pretty much self-explanatory. When it says Noah was ["the eighth person,"]{.class_s35R} it means he was the eighth generation from Adam.

The second case is Lot (vss. 6--8). Notice that when Jesus discusses the Tribulation, He uses the same two examples. ["But as the days of Noe were, so shall also the coming of the Son of man be"]{.class_s35R} (Matt. 24:37), ["Likewise also as it was in the days of Lot\...Even thus shall it be in the day when the Son of man is revealed"]{.class_s35R} (Luke 17:28--30).

In both cases you have a man, who represents a body of saved people in the future, who warns about coming judgment. Noah was ["a preacher of righteousness"]{.class_s35R} while Lot was a backslider who ["seemed as one that mocked"]{.class_s35R} (Gen. 19:14). Both of them were taken out of the way of the judgment, so the picture is that of [a rapture.]{.class_s35S}

So you have [two pictures ]{.class_s35S}here: one is the Body of Christ that witnesses to a lost world and is caught up in a pre-Tribulation rapture [before ]{.class_s35S}the Lord sends His judgment on the earth during the Tribulation. The other is a group of people who witness to a world steeped in idolatry and terrible wickedness during the Tribulation but are caught up in a post-Tribulation rapture [before Christ personally shows up]{.class_s35S} to execute judgment on the []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_451}Antichrist and False Prophet (Rev. 19) and the nations (Matt. 25). The latter is the teaching in Matthew 24 and Luke 17.

Now, Lot will forever stand in Scripture as a type of a backslidden Christian who loses everything at the Judgment Seat of Christ. If you listen to this modern preaching by some well-known evangelists, you would swear that no one could be saved and do what Lot did. But God knew Lot and described him as ["just"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 7), ["righteous"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 8), and ["godly"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 9). Of course, you would never have known that had the Lord not revealed it to you in 2 Peter.

Brethren, one of the surprises that will hit you when you get to Heaven is the people who will be there whom you didn't [think ]{.class_s35S}would have made it.

Another will be the ones who [aren't]{.class_s35S} there whom you were [sure ]{.class_s35S}would have made it!

Now, you look at the life of Lot. Lot left Abraham bound for the well-watered plains of Sodom. When the angels came to destroy the city, Lot was sitting in the gate as one of the town's judges. When it came time to leave, the angels had to drag Lot out because he tarried too long. Wouldn't you gather from all of that that Lot got along well in Sodom and was living it up down there?

But that was not the case. The Bible says that Lot's soul was ["vexed"]{.class_s35R} by the wicked things he saw and heard. He was upset; it bothered him; [it hurt him. ]{.class_s35S}Lot may have made a "killing" on beef, and he may have been "upwardly mobile" socially; but spiritually, he was miserable.

You need to remember that, brethren, when you see some of these professing Christians like Johnny Cash and Glenn Campbell who try to keep one foot in the church and the other in the world. Those fellows are some of the most miserable critters on the face of the earth. When Johnny Cash died, he had a face just like the one I draw in my sermon on "[The Wasted Life]{.class_s35S}." []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_452}That's a sermon about a [lost man ]{.class_s35S}who grows old and rejects Christ. I don't think Johnny Cash was lost, but that double-living took its toll on his [face]{.class_s35S}, boy!

If all the Christians rejected me tomorrow, I couldn't go back to the old life. It would bother me too much. I'm "rurnt" (Southern for [ruined]{.class_s35S}) on that Book, man. I couldn't take the dirty jokes or the foul language. I'd be afraid that I would laugh at the wrong thing and ruin my testimony.

Before leaving this passage, note how the word ["conversation"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 7) is defined in the very next verse. In verse 8, conversation encompasses both ["seeing and hearing."]{.class_s35R} So it's not just the talk as the world defines the word, and it's not just the lifestyle as the Christian scholars would have you believe. It's both.

9 The Lord knoweth how to deliver the godly out of temptations, and to reserve the unjust unto the day of judgment to be punished:

10 But chiefly them that walk after the flesh in the lust of uncleanness, and despise government. Presumptuous are they, selfwilled, they are not afraid to speak evil of dignities.

11 Whereas angels, which are greater in power and might, bring not railing accusation against them before the Lord.

Now, look at how that word ["godly"]{.class_s35R} is used in verse 9. That's a reference to Noah and Lot. One got drunk and passed out naked in his tent and was violated by his youngest son, and the other got drunk twice and committed incest with each of his two surviving daughters. That's how the word ["godly"]{.class_s35R} is used in the Scriptures.

When men like John R. Rice, Curtis Hutson, and Bob Jones III talk about "godly" scholars and "godly" faculty members and []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_453}"godly" men, you need to keep [that ]{.class_s35S}in mind. Being "godly" is no particular commendation. A saved bum down at the rescue mission, who still has a problem with bay rum, is just as "godly" as any faculty member of any Christian college you know. In fact, the saved "rummy" is probably more [honest]{.class_s35S} when it comes to [faith and belief in the Scriptures.]{.class_s35S}

Notice the division, in verse 9, that the Lord makes in mankind. The division is those who belong to Him (["the godly"]{.class_s35R}) and those who don't (["the unjust"]{.class_s35R}). If the ["godly"]{.class_s35R} compromise with sin and give in to sin and have their lives ruined by sin, the Lord will still deliver them as He did Lot. But ["the unjust"]{.class_s35R} are reserved ["unto the day of judgment to be punished."]{.class_s35R} The New Testament application is John 3:18. ["He that believeth on him is not condemned: but he that believeth not is condemned already."]{.class_s35R}

Now, whenever you get to preaching on the Sodomites, there is always some weak, think-skinned Christian who will pipe up and say, "We shouldn't single out this one sin; after all, sin is sin in God's sight." They say that so the queers won't label them as ["homophobes."]{.class_s35S} (I tell them that I'm not homophobic---fear of queers; I have ["homonausea"]{.class_s35S}---queers make me [sick!]{.class_s35S})

But let's just face facts, shall we. God never burned a population to the ground for stealing paper clips from the office. He never drowned a society out for calling in "sick" for work when they wanted to put in eighteen holes[ on the golf course]{.class_s35S} that day.  God won't kill over two billion Gentiles (Rev. 9:18) for [those ]{.class_s35S}kinds of sins.

When the Lord talks about punishing the unjust in the way He did in Noah's day and Lot's day, what He has in mind is verse 10: ["But chiefly them that WALK AFTER THE FLESH in the LUST OF UNCLEANNESS, and DESPISE GOVERNMENT."]{.class_s35R}

Sodomites not only ["walk after the flesh in the lust of uncleanness,"]{.class_s35R} they are [completely ]{.class_s35S}and [totally controlled ]{.class_s35S}by the flesh and its lusts.

When America accepted the Kinsey Report in 1948 and began to take all of the restrictions off sex and began to pursue pleasure at any cost, it slit its spiritual throat from ear to ear. [God won't tolerate any society that lives the way America has been living for the past fifty years.]{.class_s35S}

["Despise government."]{.class_s35R} That's where your modern anti-tax movement and militia movements lead. It's a Satanic movement made to break up churches, sell their property, and jail their pastors and members. (See comments on Rom. 13:1--5 in that Commentary.)

The cross reference to the rest of verse 10 and verse 11 is Jude 8--9, and we have covered the material in that Commentary.

12 But these, as natural brute beasts, made to be taken and destroyed, speak evil of the things that they understand not; and shall utterly perish in their own corruption;

13 And shall receive the reward of unrighteousness, as they that count it pleasure to riot in the day time. Spots they are and blemishes, sporting themselves with their own deceivings while they feast with you;

14 Having eyes full of adultery, and that cannot cease from sin; beguiling unstable souls: an heart they have exercised with covetous practices; cursed children:

["The unjust\...that walk after the flesh in the lust of uncleanness"]{.class_s35R} are compared to ["natural brute beasts" ]{.class_s35R}in verse 12. Like ["brute beasts,"]{.class_s35R} they abide by the "law of the jungle"---me first, you next (["presumptuous\...self-willed,"]{.class_s35R} []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_455}vs. 10). Like ["brute beasts,"]{.class_s35R} they will take advantage of any weakness in leadership to have their own way (["dispise government\...speak evil of dignities,"]{.class_s35R} vs. 10).

A "brute beast" is preoccupied with self-preservation, self-gratification, and self-propagation. Those are the marks of an [unsaved ]{.class_s35S}man (Matt. 6:31--32). If all you accomplish on this earth is to stay alive and well, to live as comfortably as you can, to satisfy your hunger and thirst, and to get married and raise a family, [you are no different than any dog, cat, rabbit, skunk, or raccoon]{.class_s35S}.

Throughout the Bible, unsaved men are compared to [wild, untamed, ferocious animals]{.class_s35S}. Men are born like wild asses (Job 11:12). The Gentiles are [dogs ]{.class_s35S}(Matt. 7:6, 15:26; Rev. 22:15). Unsaved politicians are [foxes ]{.class_s35S}(Luke 13:32). Unsaved religious leaders are [snakes ]{.class_s35S}(Matt. 23:33) and [wolves ]{.class_s35S}(Acts 20:29). Such people are ["made to be taken and destroyed."]{.class_s35R}

Paul says, ["If after the manner of men I have fought with beasts at Ephesus"]{.class_s35R} (1 Cor. 15:32), in reference to the riot in Acts 19:23--41. When Paul remembered one of those ["beasts,"]{.class_s35R} Alexander (Acts 19:33--34) the coppersmith (2 Tim. 4:14), he never "showed him the love of Christ" or prayed for his salvation. He said, ["Alexander the coppersmith did me much evil: the Lord reward him according to his works."]{.class_s35R}

The ["riot"]{.class_s35R} of verse 13 could refer to civil disturbances like Watts and Los Angeles, for Peter just finished describing these false teachers as those that ["despise government."]{.class_s35R} But the more likely meaning is to ["riotous living"]{.class_s35R} (Luke 15:13). We have commented on this under Romans 13:13 and 1 Peter 4:4 (which see in those Commentaries).

Verse 14: ["Having eyes full of adultery."]{.class_s35R} That's not the physical act itself. It's Matthew 5:28. ["Whosoever looketh on []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_456}a woman to lust after her lath committed adultery with her already in his heart."]{.class_s35R}

Some of the brethren who would never have a divorced and remarried preacher in their pulpit because they believe he is an "adulterer" are very careful to cover up their own adultery in this regard.

["Cursed children."]{.class_s35R} Now, every unsaved person is a "cursed child." Every human being is born into this world as a child of [wrath ]{.class_s35S}(Eph. 2:3). When they get old enough to know what sin is, every one of them becomes a "[child of disobedience]{.class_s35R}" (Eph. 2:2). If any man, woman, or child does not have God as his Father through faith in the Lord Jesus Christ (John 1:12), then the [Devil ]{.class_s35S}is his father (see John 8:44 and comments in that Commentary). Every unsaved person is a child of pride whose king is ["a great red dragon"]{.class_s35R} (Job 41:34 and context cf. Rev. 12:3), and if he never receives Christ, he is a ["child of hell"]{.class_s35R} (Matt. 23:15).

But you see, right now, during the Church Age, you can [change]{.class_s35S} your family. [The moment you receive Christ, your lineage changes]{.class_s35S}. You receive a new birth into a new family (Eph. 2). God adopts you as one of [His sons ]{.class_s35S}(Gal. 4:5).

The implication in verse 14 is that these ["cursed children"]{.class_s35R} are [stuck]{.class_s35S} in that state. In the Tribulation, it seems that there are groups of people whom God intends to damn with no hope of salvation.

That's not true [now ]{.class_s35S}(see 2 Pet. 3:9). Right now, the Lord offers salvation freely to anyone who will repent and receive Christ. But once the Rapture takes place and the Body of Christ is caught up to Heaven, things are different.

There is one group of people who heard the Gospel in the Church Age and rejected it. Second Thessalonians 2:11--12 says of this group: ["And for this cause God shall send them strong delusion, that they should believe a lie: ]{.class_s35R}[That []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_457}they all might be damned who believed not the truth]{.class_s35W-0}[, but had pleasure in unrighteousness."]{.class_s35R}

Then there are a group of Jews who believe on Christ and are saved, but they fall back into idolatry like the children of Israel who apostatized in the book of Judges. When they do that, ["it is impossible\...]{.class_s35R}[if they fall away]{.class_s35W-0}[, to renew them again unto repentance"]{.class_s35R} (Heb. 6:4--6 and comments in that Commentary).

If a Jew loses his salvation in the Tribulation, it is impossible for him to get it back.

A third group is anyone who receives the mark of the beast or worships the Antichrist and his image. Revelation 14:10 says of these people, ["The same shall drink of the wine of the wrath of God, which is poured out without mixture into the cup of his indignation; and he shall be tormented with fire and brimstone in the presence of the holy angels, and in the presence of the Lamb."]{.class_s35R}

The false prophets and teachers of 2 Peter 2 are the fourth group whom God intends to damn in the Tribulation. Peter likened them back in verse 12 to ["natural brute beasts, MADE to be taken and destroyed."]{.class_s35R}

15 Which have forsaken the right way, and are gone astray, following the way of Balaam the son of Bosor, who loved the wages of unrighteousness;

16 But was rebuked for his iniquity: the dumb ass speaking with man's voice forbad the madness of the prophet.

Balaam is the Gentile prophet mentioned in Numbers 22, 23, and 24. He was hired by Balak, king of Moab, to curse the children of Israel before they entered the Promised Land.

He appears [three times ]{.class_s35S}in the New Testament: verse 15, Jude 11, and Revelation 2:14. There are three things about him []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_458}for which you are told to look out: his ["way"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 15), his ["error"]{.class_s35R} (Jude 11), and his ["doctrine"]{.class_s35R} (Rev. 2:14).

I have commented in detail on ["the error of Balaam"]{.class_s35R} and ["the doctrine of Balaam"]{.class_s35R} in my commentaries on Jude and Revelation. Briefly, ["the error of Balaam"]{.class_s35R} was returning to Balak with a way of cursing Israel when God wouldn't let Balaam curse a people who had His[ imputed righteousness]{.class_s35S}. ["The doctrine of Balaam"]{.class_s35R} was teaching Israel to commit fornication and intermarry with the heathen women of Moab and to offer sacrifices to their false gods.

But before that, Balaam had a ["way"]{.class_s35R} that led to his ["error"]{.class_s35R} and ["doctrine."]{.class_s35R} That ["way"]{.class_s35R} is defined in verse 15. It was loving ["the wages of unrighteousness."]{.class_s35R} He didn't love[ the unrighteousness]{.class_s35S}. He didn't love the wrong thing. He loved [the payment ]{.class_s35S}he would get from doing the wrong thing. He loved it so much that he would cut two-thirds of the message God gave him (Num. 22:13) and ignore half of God's instructions to him (Num. 22:20--21) [just to get the money.]{.class_s35S}

["But was rebuked for his iniquity: the dumb ass speaking with man's voice forbade the madness of the prophet"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 16). Which just goes to show you that a ["dumb ass"]{.class_s35R} is smarter than a backslidden preacher.

Although Balaam did get angry with his beast in Numbers 22:27, ["the madness of the prophet"]{.class_s35R} refers to the fact that covetousness drove Balaam crazy. Three times that ass avoided ["the angel of the ]{.class_s35R}[Lord]{.class_s35X-0}[,"]{.class_s35R} and if Balaam's mind hadn't been so clouded with greed, he would have realized what was happening. But sin never leaves you in your right mind (Luke 15:17).

17 These are wells without water, clouds that are carried with a tempest: to whom the mist of darkness is reserved for ever.

18 For when they speak great swelling words of vanity, they allure through the lusts of the flesh, []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_459}through much wantonness, those that were clean escaped from them who live in error.

19 While they promise them liberty, they themselves are the servants of corruption: for of whom a man is overcome, of the same is he brought in bondage.

I have already commented on the material in verse 17 under Jude 12--13. And although Peter says ["wells without water"]{.class_s35R} and Jude says ["clouds\...without water,"]{.class_s35R} the illustration is the same: these false prophets and false teachers are devoid of the water of life (John 4:14) and can't give the ["living water" ]{.class_s35R}to a sinner because they don't have it themselves.

Note in verse 18 how they ensnare the sinner. First they appeal to his pride. ["They speak great swelling words of vanity."]{.class_s35R} Those are big words, that mean nothing, to flatter you and make you think highly of yourself.

Here's a good example of ["great swelling words."]{.class_s35R} It's from a preacher named Gordon Carpenter who had just gotten his Masters' Degree from some Southern Baptist seminary. He came out with this during a message he was preaching at a church in Panama City.

"It is [pertinent ]{.class_s35S}to [scrutinize ]{.class_s35S}secular history minutely and [delve out]{.class_s35S} into the [magnetic ]{.class_s35S}attraction of the [threefold aspect]{.class_s35S} in the prophetic realm to integrate the [apocalyptic books]{.class_s35S} into a perfect monomy. The insidious inexorably neglect the [panoramic consummation]{.class_s35S} of the prophetic view for mankind. There is neither discrepancy nor incongruity in the [veracity ]{.class_s35S}or the [authenticity ]{.class_s35S}of the transition of this [cataclysmic ]{.class_s35S}dispensation.

Those are ["great swelling words."]{.class_s35R} I don't know whom the fellow was trying to impress, but all he did was make a big fool out of himself. What he said was, "We ought to look []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_460}carefully at Daniel and not doubt it." He said that world history will prove that the book of Daniel is true. He said you ought to take the book of Daniel and the book of Revelation together.

Now, anyone can take highly technical language and bamboozle people who aren't familiar with the jargon. I guarantee you that I could tie the most brilliant neurosurgeon in Pensacola in verbal knots to where he would have no idea what I said. All I have to do is start talking about the ultima and penult and the iota subscriptum and the antepenult and supralapsarianism and sublapsarianism and infralapsarianism and dynamic equivalence and the Hesychian text and the Boharic and the Sahidic manuscripts and miniscules and uncials and kephalia; he wouldn't know which end was up, man.

[That is one way of deceiving you]{.class_s35Z}. The other method they use is an appeal to your fleshy desires. ["They allure through the lusts of the flesh, through much wantonness."]{.class_s35R}

["Those that were clean escaped from them who live in error."]{.class_s35R} What you have here is a bunch of people who have [temporarily ]{.class_s35S}escaped error and have cleaned up. When that happens, these false prophets and teachers lure them back into the error through [flattery and lust.]{.class_s35S}

If you have ever done any personal work, then you know what that verse is talking about. You can be dealing with a person at work or in your neighborhood, and you will get that person either up to the point of getting saved, or you will lead the person to Christ and get ready to disciple them. Just about that time, up will show a Charismatic or a Campbellite or a Seventh-day Adventist or a Jehovah's Witness and blow the whole thing to pieces. [That's a demonic spirit; those people are "led."]{.class_s35S}

A hyperdispensational church here in town used to send its girls over to our church to start [dating ]{.class_s35S}the young men here at PBI. Several of those young men ended up marrying those girls, dropping out of Bible school, and started  attending the Dry []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_461}Cleaner church. [They never did anything else for God the rest of their lives]{.class_s35S}.

Now, how do these false prophets and teachers convince these folks to come back to what they escaped? Verse 19: ["They promise them LIBERTY."]{.class_s35R} That's the "buzz word."

King Louis in France was too strict and too tyrannical. So the cry went up, "[Liberty, Equality, Fraternity!]{.class_s35S}"; and in came the Reign of Terror and the Napoleonic wars.

The Communists are going to "liberate" the proletariat from the bourgeoise, so you have a revolution in Russia and Cuba and China to overthrow the oppressive governments and replace them with [military dictatorships ]{.class_s35S}run by Lenin, Stalin, Mao Tse-tung, and Castro.

Russia wants to "liberate" Eastern Europe, so it invades Hungary and Czechoslovakia. Martin Luther King Jr. and the NAACP want to "liberate" the black man, so they send the [troops ]{.class_s35S}into Mississippi and they pass the Civil Rights Bill of 1964. What's the result? [An exploding crime rate, rampant violence in the schools, and out-of-control VD, abortion, and illegitimate births]{.class_s35S}.

You had better watch out for anybody with the moral standards of a Rousseau or Stalin or Castro or Martin Luther King Jr. or a Ted Kennedy promising you [liberty ]{.class_s35S}to do anything. They are slaves to their own sinful passions, and they want to enslave [you. ]{.class_s35S}["]{.class_s35R}[They themselves are the servants of corruption]{.class_s35W-0}[: for of whom a man is overcome, of the same is he brought in bondage."]{.class_s35R}

The thing that made the American Revolution for "liberty" different from all of those other fiascoes was that its leaders were [white, straight, Protestant males]{.class_s35S} who [believed]{.class_s35S} and [practised the Bible. ]{.class_s35S}The liberty for which they fought was the liberty to worship God [apart from the dictates of the State. ]{.class_s35S}When they set up a government, they set up a government based upon the []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_462}philosophy that every man, including themselves, was a [sinner ]{.class_s35S}who needed his [baser instincts]{.class_s35S} brought into check, and yet, every man was also a free moral agent answerable directly [to God]{.class_s35S} and needed the freedom to carry out his Maker's will.

When they educated the future leaders of the Republic, they didn't use Mao's [Red Book]{.class_s35S} or Marx's [Communist Manifesto]{.class_s35S} or Engel's [Das Kapital]{.class_s35S} or Tom Paine's [Common Sense]{.class_s35S} or [Pravda]{.class_s35S} or any other like trash. [They taught the Bible and the hymnal in their schools, and all textbooks were based on those two sources.]{.class_s35S}

If anybody offers you liberty [on those conditions,]{.class_s35S} then you are getting a pretty good deal. Otherwise, forget it.

20 For if after they have escaped the pollutions of the world through the knowledge of the Lord and Saviour Jesus Christ, they are again entangled therein, and overcome, the latter end is worse with them than the beginning.

21 For it had been better for them not to have known the way of righteousness, than, after they have known it, to turn from the holy commandment delivered unto them.

22 But it is happened unto them according to the true proverb, The dog is turned to his own vomit again; and the sow that was washed to her wallowing in the mire.

Now, what is the case of these false prophets and teachers? Verse 20:

1\) ["They have escaped the pollutions of the world."]{.class_s35R} They straightened up and got cleaned up.

2\) ["Through the knowledge of the Lord and Saviour Jesus Christ."]{.class_s35R} Notice it is not ["the knowledge of OUR Lord Jesus Christ"]{.class_s35R} as it was back in 2 Peter 1:8. Peter doesn't []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_463}include himself with these people in any way, at any time. The implication is not only that they aren't saved, but they never were saved.

3\) ["They are again entangled therein and overcome."]{.class_s35R} They go back to what they left.

These people have the truth preached to them, which in the Tribulation is salvation by faith in Jesus Christ [and ]{.class_s35S}keeping the commandments (Rev. 12:17 and 14:12). They start [keeping the commandments]{.class_s35S} and living right, but they never do personally receive Christ. They ["]{.class_s35R}[turn from the holy commandment]{.class_s35W-0}[ delivered unto them"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 21). In this case, ["]{.class_s35R}[the holy commandment]{.class_s35W-0}["]{.class_s35R} was a reference to 1 John 3:23. ["]{.class_s35R}[And this is his commandment]{.class_s35W-0}[, That we should believe on the name of his Son Jesus Christ, and love one another, as he gave us commandment."]{.class_s35R}

So the ["knowledge"]{.class_s35R} they had of Jesus Christ was the knowledge [Satan ]{.class_s35S}and the [devils ]{.class_s35S}have (Mark 1:24; Acts 16:17, 19:15). When it comes to the deity of Jesus Christ, all the devils are ["Fundamentalists]{.class_s35S}." It doesn't do them any more good than [believing in one God]{.class_s35S} (James 2:19).

One of the surest ways that you know the false prophets and teachers were never saved is verse 22. [The false prophets were never anything but dogs. ]{.class_s35S}They weren't converted from a dog to a sheep, then back to a dog upon losing salvation. The false prophet was a [dog ]{.class_s35S}who reacted to his own puke (["the pollutions of the world"]{.class_s35R} that he had gotten out of his system) as any dog would.

The false teacher didn't change from a hog to a sheep and then back to a hog. [She was washed and then went back to wallow in her filth as any pig will do.]{.class_s35S}

Peter says that ["the latter end is worse with them than the beginning"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 20), and ["it had been better for them []{#c2W0.xhtml_page_464}not to have known the way of righteousness"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 21). Why? Because now they have no chance to be saved.

Evidently, in the Tribulation, the Lord gives these false prophets and teachers [one chance]{.class_s35S} (and one chance only) to be saved. Rather than trusting Christ and then trying to ["endure to the end,"]{.class_s35R} they rely completely on their own self-righteousness. They are quickly drawn from their clean life by their former lusts and go back to the old life. The only problem, at that point, is now they are [permanently damned]{.class_s35S}, whereas before they had a chance.

These false prophets and false teachers are like the fellow in Matthew 12:43--45. The man was [freed ]{.class_s35S}from a demonic spirit. He was [clean ]{.class_s35S}but had no Holy Spirit to take the place of the devil that left. That devil will wander about for a while and then come back to "check" that guy out. If there's no new resident in his former "apartment," so the demon will go get seven of his buddies and move back in, and that guy is in worse shape than if he had never had the one devil removed to begin with.

That is the case of these false prophets and teachers. Not only do they seal their fate by rejecting Christ and returning to the old life; [they are more wicked than they were before.]{.class_s35S}

[]{#c307.xhtml}

## Chapter 3 {.heading_s3A-0}

3:1 This second epistle, beloved, I now write unto you; in both which I stir up your pure minds by way of remembrance:

2 That ye may be mindful of the words which were spoken before by the holy prophets, and of the commandment of us the apostles of the Lord and Saviour:

3 Knowing this first, that there shall come in the last days scoffers, walking after their own lusts,

4 And saying, Where is the promise of his coming? for since the fathers fell asleep, all things continue as they were from the beginning of the creation.

Now we're back on track where Peter started in chapter 1 (["remembrance,"]{.class_s35R} vs. 1 cf. 2 Pet. 1:12--15). The doctrine Peter is going to call to your ["remembrance"]{.class_s35R} is the doctrine of the Second Coming, but as in all the General Epistles you have to be careful.

When Peter defines the [Second Coming ]{.class_s35S}in chapter 3, he never describes the [Rapture of the Church]{.class_s35S} about which you read in 1 Corinthians 15 and 1 Thessalonians 4. He doesn't even describe the Second Advent that John saw in Revelation 19.

The coming of Christ in 2 Peter 3 [is connected with the destruction of the earth at the end of the Millennium, the White Throne Judgment, and the creation of the New Heavens and New Earth from Revelation]{.class_s35S} 20:11--21:1. Look at verses 7--13 in 2 Peter 3.

Poor Marvin Rosenthal got so confused by these verses that he had the Rapture take place in the second half of the Tribulation after the Antichrist's image has been set up in a rebuilt temple and the mark is given, [twenty-one months before the Second Advent]{.class_s35S}. He confused the 2nd Advent with the end of []{#c307.xhtml_page_466}the Millenium which is 1,000 years later. You talk about a mess: that's a mess!

Verse 2 divides the chapter into two sections. The first is ["the words which were spoken before by the holy prophets."]{.class_s35R} This section runs from verse 5 to verse 13.

The second section is ["the commandment of us the apostles of the Lord and Saviour."]{.class_s35R} That section runs from verse 14 to the end of the book. ["The apostles,"]{.class_s35R} in that section, specifically are Peter (vs. 1) and the Apostle Paul (vss. 15--16).

Notice in verse 2 that you are to be ["mindful of the words"]{.class_s35R} of Scripture; not just the thoughts, doctrines, or fundamentals. It is not just the [word]{.class_s35S} of God; it is the [words. ]{.class_s35S}Christ said it was ["every word"]{.class_s35R} (Matt. 4:4).

Verse 3 puts the subject matter in ["the last days."]{.class_s35R} That is a time that covers the Great Apostasy immediately before the Rapture (2 Tim. 3:1) to the end of the Tribulation. If I had to set a date for when they began, I would have to say between 1885--1901. That is when the British set aside their [AV]{.class_s35S} for Westcott and Hort's [Revised Version]{.class_s35S} and the Americans turned in their [KJV]{.class_s35S} for an [American Standard Version.]{.class_s35S}

Apostasy didn't begin with unsaved Liberals. It began with Bible-rejecting Christians.

["There shall come in the last days scoffers\...saying, Where is the promise of his coming?"]{.class_s35R} (vss. 3--4). So ["in the last days,"]{.class_s35R} it will become more and more common for men to mock the Bible and make fun of the Lord and ridicule prophecy.

I witnessed to an old man once and asked him, "Don't you want to be ready for the Lord to come back, dad?"

He replied, "Oh, that's nonsense. I remember my [grandfather ]{.class_s35S}talking about that, about the Lord coming."

That's a good example of a scoffer. He figured since his [granddad ]{.class_s35S}talked about it and his granddad before him, and since it hasn't happened yet, that [it won't happen]{.class_s35S}.

But you can't restrict that verse to just lost folks. As we get closer and closer to the Rapture, and it seems that the Lord just tarries longer, more and more Christians are giving up their ["blessed hope"]{.class_s35R} (Titus 2:13). [They have stopped looking for the Lord to come back.]{.class_s35S}

They mock the [Scofield Reference Bible;]{.class_s35S} specifically those notes and references that deal with prophecy. They make light [of prophecy]{.class_s35S} and try to overemphasize the [ministry]{.class_s35S}. They look for the [Antichrist ]{.class_s35S}and his one-world government to show up and for the temple to be rebuilt. They are always on the look out for the [mark of the beast]{.class_s35S} to show up.

I have taught the Bible for nearly fifty years now. I know where the [Scofield Bible]{.class_s35S} is wrong, but when it comes to the [general outline]{.class_s35S} of Bible prophecy, Scofield has it "right on the money."

I appreciate the ministries God has given me. I don't use the Lord's return as an excuse for being lazy.

I know that the Antichrist, the False Prophet, the One World Church, and the One World Government are going to show up. I don't kid myself. If the Lord doesn't come back soon and if I don't die, I know that we Bible-believing Christians are in for some rough times.

But even though I know all of that, I don't lose sight of what the Lord told me to do. I was commanded ["to wait for his Son from heaven\...even Jesus, which delivered us from the wrath to come"]{.class_s35R} (1 Thess. 1:10).

While I am teaching and preaching that Book and believing what it says, and while I am trying to win the lost to Christ and send the Gospel around the world; while I am doing all of that, at the same time, I am ["looking for that blessed []{#c307.xhtml_page_468}hope, and the glorious appearing of the great God and our Saviour Jesus Christ"]{.class_s35R} (Titus 2:13). I was commanded to [watch]{.class_s35S} in regards to His coming (Mark 13:35--37; 1 Thess. 5:6), and brother, I'm watching!

["For since the fathers fell asleep, all things continue as they were from the beginning of the creation."]{.class_s35R} That's a doctrine known as [uniformitarianism]{.class_s35S}; it is the basis for the [theory of evolution]{.class_s35S}. The idea is that since the world began, only natural forces have been slowly forming everything the way we see them today.

If you go to the Grand Canyon or Niagara Falls, the park rangers will tell you that what you see was formed over millions (sometimes billions) of years by the flow of water. That is because uniformitarian geology and evolution is [the official stance of the United States government.]{.class_s35S}

They do not take into account a universal flood in Genesis 1:2 or a universal flood in Genesis 7. Those are [catastrophic events ]{.class_s35S}that caused geological formations to develop quickly.

That is known as ["catastrophic geology."]{.class_s35S} It can be seen today in the aftermath of the eruption of Mount St. Helens in Washington State ([1980]{.class_s35S}). After that volcano deposited tons of ash around the mountain and after torrential rains fell, creating massive mud slides from quick erosion, scientists discovered a one-fortieth scale model of the Grand Canyon that had been cut in the mud (by "Mother Nature," no doubt. Don't you know).

Do you think the National Park System changed what it said about the development of the Grand Canon after that discovery? [Of course not!]{.class_s35S} Men don't believe evolution because it is scientifically accurate; they accept evolution [because they don't want to give account to their Creator]{.class_s35S}.

Every dating method used by evolutionists to get these huge eras of time is based on the assumption that the composition of the atmosphere and the rate of [nuclear decay ]{.class_s35S}are "constants" []{#c307.xhtml_page_469}that never change. That is the basis for the Carbon-14 dating method and the Potassium-Argon dating method. The older a thing is in time, the more unreliable those methods are.

The reason for that is an event like the Flood dramatically [changed the atmosphere]{.class_s35S}, which in turn allowed various cosmic and solar rays to enter that had not been able to enter before. Exposure to these new radiations changed the r[ate of nuclear decay]{.class_s35S} in the materials used in these dating methods. Also, the movement of large deposits of water [changed the amount of the original material]{.class_s35S} that would decay. Scientists today [assume]{.class_s35S} an amount of original material based on the amount of decayed material and the present decay rate.

It's the same kind of circular reasoning that geologists use to date rocks and fossils from the strata in which they are found. Using current sedimentation rates, they calculate how old a strata should be. Then they assign that age to every fossil found [in that strata]{.class_s35S}. So a fossil is assigned an age based on the strata, and wherever that type of fossil is found in the world, the strata of rock from which it was taken is assigned an age [based on the fossil]{.class_s35S}.

That kind of reasoning is symbolized by taking your index finger, pointing it at the side of your head, and [making circles with it]{.class_s35S}. Do you see why an event like the Flood messes up the scientists so? If the sediment was laid down within a year (Gen. 7:13 cf. Gen. 8:13), all over the earth at the same time, that would bring ages of sixty-five million to four billion years down to five thousand to ten thousand years. Any evolutionist would agree that that is far too little time, even with "biological predestination" and "sudden explosions of life," to account for everything we see today. The only reasonable conclusion, at that point, would be that the universe was made by an [intelligent Designer]{.class_s35S}; and all the mathematical, statistical, anthropological, []{#c307.xhtml_page_470}historical, and scientific evidence points to the Genesis 1 account as the only accurate historical account of the creation.

People do have a time of it, don't they?

5 For this they willingly are ignorant of, that by the word of God the heavens were of old, and the earth standing out of the water and in the water:

6 Whereby the world that then was, being overflowed with water, perished:

7 But the heavens and the earth, which are now, by the same word are kept in store, reserved unto fire against the day of judgment and perdition of ungodly men.

["For this they are willingly ignorant"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 5). Watch out! The ["they"]{.class_s35R} of verse 5 refers back to the uniformitarians in verse 4. You can expect them to be ignorant of what follows. They believe the entire universe came from a marble-sized "egg" (Big Bang Theory). But what you don't expect is for a bunch of [Christians ]{.class_s35S}who profess to [believe ]{.class_s35S}in the Bible and believe in creation to be ignorant. Sadly enough, though, [that ]{.class_s35S}is exactly the case.

["That by the word of God the heavens were of old, and the earth standing out of the water and in the water: Whereby the world that then was, being over flowed with water, perished"]{.class_s35R} (vss. 5--6).

And out goes Henry Morris, Gary Parker, Duane Gish, Kent Hovind, Ken Ham, and the rest of the Creation Research Institute. Every one locates that verse in Genesis 7 as Noah's Flood. [Not one of them got it right]{.class_s35S}.

The context is ["the beginning of the creation"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 4), and the comparison is to the destruction and recreation of the universe in Revelation 20--21 (vss. 10--13). [It couldn't possibly be the Flood of Noah's day.]{.class_s35S}

If that weren't enough, look at verse 5: ["the earth standing out of the water and in the water."]{.class_s35R} That's [not ]{.class_s35S}the earth of Genesis 6. The earth in that verse is the entire planet; it's not the ["dry land"]{.class_s35R} of Genesis 1:9.

In verses 5 and 6, part of the planet is ["in the water,"]{.class_s35R} and part of it is ["out of the water."]{.class_s35R} In Genesis 1:9, the waters were gathered together [on]{.class_s35S} the earth; the earth wasn't [in]{.class_s35S} them. In Genesis 7:17, the Flood waters were ["upon the earth"]{.class_s35R}; again, the earth was not [in]{.class_s35S} them.

The waters of Noah's Flood are said to have been ["upon the earth"]{.class_s35R} (Gen. 7:17), and to have ["prevailed"]{.class_s35R} and ["covered"]{.class_s35R} the earth (Gen. 7:19), but never to have ["overflowed"]{.class_s35R} it.

An overflow is what takes place when an object is [pushed]{.class_s35S} beneath water. The water [flows over]{.class_s35S} the sides of the object.

Now, all of this has to do with what is known as the "gap theory." The "gap theory" is the teaching that something took place between Genesis 1:1 and Genesis 1:2 that is not explained there but can be inferred from other places in the Scriptures such as Isaiah 14 and Ezekiel 28.

The creationists like to call it a "theory" because it can't be "proven" scientifically. Of course, neither can the creation itself, according to the "scientific method" (i.e., for an event to be accepted as a "scientific fact," it must be observed by man and repeatable under controlled conditions).

Creationists don't care for the doctrine of the "gap" because some believers [in the past ]{.class_s35S}have used it to explain the dinosaurs and the incredible ages the early evolutionists were proposing for the earth. The creationists insist that such a gap would violate Romans 5:12 because there would have been death before Adam.

Let's get some things straight about this, shall we. First, the Bible never says that there was anything besides ["the sons of God"]{.class_s35R} in Genesis 1:1 (Job 38:4--7). If the flood of Genesis 1:2 did []{#c307.xhtml_page_472}kill off animal life like the dinosaurs, that certainly would have nothing to do with the present creation. Adam was the [federal head ]{.class_s35S}(Gen. 1:28) over the creation of Genesis 1:3--27. That is why sin could not enter the world through Satan and Eve (who certainly did sin before Adam). That did not cause Genesis 1:2-3.

You see, the creationists forgot to read that part of Romans 5:12. Not only did death enter the world through Adam, [sin did as well]{.class_s35S}. Anybody reading the account of Genesis 3 knows that Eve was the first human being ever to sin on this earth.

Finally, if Noah's Flood interfered with the dating methods of the evolutionists, what do you think the flood of Genesis 1:2 would have done? Even some of the dating methods used by the creationists to prove a "young earth" sometimes give dates from 10,000 to 1,000,000 years. The creationists say the earth hasn't been around for more than 6,000 years. What do you do with that "extra time"?

The flood of Genesis 1:2 causes as much trouble for the creationists as Noah's Flood does for the evolutionists.

Now let's go back to the Biblical facts. In Genesis 1, God created ["worlds"]{.class_s35R} (Heb. 1:2, 11:3). Second Peter 3 defines a [world]{.class_s35S} as the entirety of creation: both ["the heavens and the earth."]{.class_s35R} The Bible distinguishes ["the world that then was"]{.class_s35R} from ["the heavens and the earth, which are now."]{.class_s35R} So the ["worlds"]{.class_s35R} that were created in Genesis 1 are the world of Genesis 1:1 (which was completely destroyed [by a flood]{.class_s35S} in Genesis 1:2), and the world of Genesis 1:3--27. Although [all flesh ]{.class_s35S}on this earth, except for those in the ark, was destroyed by a flood in Genesis 7, the world itself, the [heavens ]{.class_s35S}that were created in Genesis 1:6--8 and 15--19 and the earth that was [recreated after]{.class_s35S} Genesis 1:3, was not completely destroyed. It will be, someday, by fire (2 Pet. 3). After it is, the Lord will recreate the world in Revelation 21, just as He did in Genesis 1:3--27.

The world of Genesis 1:1 was destroyed as a result of the rebellion of Satan in Isaiah 14 and Ezekiel 28, and the Bible likens the earth that is judged in the Tribulation as a result of Satan's rebellion in that earth that was flooded in Genesis 1:2 as a result of his rebellion then (Jer. 4:23). See comments on Genesis 1:2 in that Commentary.

8 But, beloved, be not ignorant of this one thing, that one day is with the Lord as a thousand years, and a thousand years as one day.

9 The Lord is not slack concerning his promise, as some men count slackness; but is longsuffering to us-ward, not willing that any should perish, but that all should come to repentance.

10 But the day of the Lord will come as a thief in the night; in the which the heavens shall pass away with a great noise, and the elements shall melt with fervent heat, the earth also and the works that are therein shall be burned up.

11 Seeing then that all these things shall be dissolved, what manner of persons ought ye to be in all holy conversation and godliness,

12 Looking for and hasting unto the coming of the day of God, wherein the heavens being on fire shall be dissolved, and the elements shall melt with fervent heat?

13 Nevertheless we, according to his promise, look for new heavens and a new earth, wherein dwelleth righteousness.

We have covered verse 8 many times before. The context is [prophecy]{.class_s35S}, not the days of creation in Genesis 1. A system of [seven ]{.class_s35S}is established through the Bible and is first set down in Genesis 2 by Moses. God works six days and rests the seventh.

Isaiah 11:10 describes the Millennial reign of Christ (1,000 years---Rev. 20:1--7) as His ["rest."]{.class_s35R} Isaiah 14:7 says that during the Millennium that ["the whole earth is at rest."]{.class_s35R} So far, you have had six thousand years of "labor" on this earth. At some point in the near future, the Lord will begin His Millennial "day" of rest.

Here is a great verse that you should memorize: verse 9. The verse states that if you go to Hell, you will be going [against the will of God]{.class_s35S}. He doesn't want you there, He didn't make it for you (Matt. 25:41), and He did all He could to [keep you out]{.class_s35S}. The decision (Rom. 10:13) is now yours.

Of course, Calvin would try to limit God's will to the elect only. The ["us-ward,"]{.class_s35R} under Calvin's system, would be "us elect." If that's the case, think how much nonsense is in this verse. God isn't ["longsuffering"]{.class_s35R} to the elect. ["Longsuffering"]{.class_s35R} implies that God gives you so much time before His patience runs out. God's patience doesn't runout at all with the "elect" under Calvin's system. [He knows that they are going to repent, they can't repent until He regenerates them,]{.class_s35S} He knows when He is going to regenerate them, and when He regenerates them they can't resist His will. How is [longsuffering ]{.class_s35S}involved in any of that, I ask you?

Now, if you are an Amillennialist and thought we were stretching things back in verse 8, look at verse 10. ["The day of the Lord"]{.class_s35R} is not a twenty-four hour day at all. It is a [prophetic day]{.class_s35S} that encompasses the Rapture of the Church (1 Thess. 5:2), the Second Advent (Zech. 14:1--5; Joel 2 cf. Rev. 16:14--15), and the destruction of the world by fire (vs. 10).

In each case, the Lord comes as a thief to "steal" something. Actually, [He is just taking back what is His,]{.class_s35S} but it is currently in the possession of someone else. In the Rapture, the Lord comes to take His children out of the world. At the Advent, the Lord comes to rescue His people Israel from the hand of the []{#c307.xhtml_page_475}Antichrist. When He destroys the universe, He takes those saints who are under siege in Jerusalem, and he empties the graves of those Gentile saints from Adam to Jesus Christ (Job 19:25--26).

["In which the heavens shall pass away with a great noise, and the elements shall melt with fervent heat, the earth also and the works that are therein shall be burned up."]{.class_s35R} You may not realize it, but right now, every atom in your body is trying to fly apart, and if they did, you would go up in a mushroom cloud just like the ones over Hiroshima and Nagasaki. The only thing that [holds them together]{.class_s35S} is the Lord Jesus Christ (Heb. 1:3; Col. 1:16--17). All He has to do is speak the word and let those atoms loose, and "up she goes"!

You talk about ["a great noise"]{.class_s35R} and ["fervent heat!"]{.class_s35R} When the Lord lets the whole universe go up in flames, you will see an atomic explosion that will make a "supernova" look like a firecracker going off.

Now, you need to "consider the latter end" of these things and keep it in mind. [Some day the whole universe is going to burn up]{.class_s35S}. Your house: it's going to burn. Your car: it's going to burn. Your back account: it will be ashes. Everything you [see]{.class_s35S} will be gone. That is why Paul said, ["the things which are seen are temporal; but the things which are not seen are eternal"]{.class_s35R} (2 Cor. 4:18). So if you are going to pour a lot of time, effort, and expenses into building a house, make sure it's your mansion in Glory (John 14:2; 1 Cor. 3:10--14), and if you are going to build up a big "nest egg," make sure it's in the bank of Heaven (Matt. 6:19--21).

Peter says, ["Seeing then that all these things shall be dissolved, what manner of persons ought ye to be in all holy conversation and godliness" ]{.class_s35R}(vs. 11). Christians should have their "priorities straight." It's not living to survive down here; it's living to prepare for "over there" in Heaven and eternity.

["Looking for and hasting unto the coming of the day of God"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 12). A Christian should be looking forward to and desiring the Lord's return. Like John, he should pray, ["Even so, come, Lord Jesus"]{.class_s35R} (Rev. 22:20).

I don't like that hillbilly song that says "Wait a little longer, please Jesus." My sentiments have always been "Hurry up a little faster, please, Jesus." Let'er rip!

Folks think I'm irreverent when I say that, but that's how I feel. I'm ready for the Lord to come back so we can finish this mess and get onto the Millennium. If there was anything I could do, without sinning, to touch off the Rapture, I would do it in a heartbeat. If the Lord ever offers to grant one prayer request I ask, you had better fasten your seatbelts, brethren, because we're taking off!

I love the beauties of the physical creation, and I enjoy all the good things God gives me down here. But when it comes to this world, [as a whole,]{.class_s35S} there is nothing down here for which I want to hang around. Someone asked me once, "How's the world treating you?" I replied, "As usual, but the Lord's been real good to me."

I figure the world owes me a living, and it's behind three payments.

Back in the early twentieth century, Haley's Comet was passing by the earth really close, and everyone was in a panic. A man said to Thomas Edison, the inventor of the light bulb, "Haley's Comet is going to crash into the earth, and the world's coming to an end." Calmly, Thomas Edison said, ["That's OK. We can do without it."]{.class_s35S}

When it comes to the ["present evil world"]{.class_s35R} (Gal. 1:4), brethren, "we can do without it."

Now, when the Bible talks about ["new heavens and a new earth"]{.class_s35R} (vs. 13), it's not talking about a [different]{.class_s35S} heavens and earth. Ecclesiastes 1:4 says, ["the earth abideth for []{#c307.xhtml_page_477}ever."]{.class_s35R} Just like the Lord used the material from the original creation (Gen. 1:1) to form the present world (Gen. 1:3--27), the Lord will use the [material ]{.class_s35S}from the universe in which we live now to form the new heavens and the new earth. He melts it down, as a refiner would gold or silver, and removes the "dross" to make a new, clean universe, untouched by sin (vs. 13).

Note that in the new creation, "righteousness" dwells in the [new heavens]{.class_s35S} as well as the [new earth. ]{.class_s35S}Isaiah 9:7 says,[ "Of the INCREASE of his government and peace there shall be NO END."]{.class_s35R} You might be able to spiritualize ["peace"]{.class_s35R} in that passage, but you can't spiritualize ["the increase of his government."]{.class_s35R} Government deals with territory. If there will be ["no end"]{.class_s35R} to ["the increase of his government,"]{.class_s35R} that means that ["his government"]{.class_s35R} goes into outer space to other planets. (See comments under Rom. 4:13 on the Gentile nations in eternity.)

14 Wherefore, beloved, seeing that ye look for such things, be diligent that ye may be found of him in peace, without spot, and blameless.

15 And account that the longsuffering of our Lord is salvation; even as our beloved brother Paul also according to the wisdom given unto him hath written unto you;

16 As also in all his epistles, speaking in them of these things; in which are some things hard to be understood, which they that are unlearned and unstable wrest, as they do also the other scriptures, unto their own destruction.

17 Ye therefore, beloved, seeing ye know these things before, beware lest ye also, being led away with the error of the wicked, fall from your own stedfastness.

18 But grow in grace, and in the knowledge of our Lord and Saviour Jesus Christ. To him be glory both now and for ever. Amen.

Now we are into the section where Peter is going to give ["the commandment of us the apostles of the Lord and Saviour,"]{.class_s35R} and if I were to sum up the passage with my own words, they would be: "Watch yourself." Make sure that when the Lord returns, He finds [you ]{.class_s35S}"doing right." In his first epistle, the Apostle John says in regards to the return of Christ for His sons, ["And every man that hath this hope in him" ]{.class_s35R}(["that blessed hope"]{.class_s35R} of Titus 2:13) ["purifieth himself, even as he is pure"]{.class_s35R} (1 John 3:3).

Peter says in verse 14, ["Be diligent."]{.class_s35R} So you are going to have to work hard at something. Down in verse 17, he says, ["beware."]{.class_s35R} So you are going to have to watch out and avoid something. So in verses 15 and 17, the doctrine of the Second Coming should lead you to do some things and to avoid others.

Now look at verse 14. ["Be diligent that ye may be found of him in peace, without spot, and blameless."]{.class_s35R} All of that is positionally true of every child of God in this age.

Romans 5:1, ["Therefore being justified by faith, we have PEACE with God through our Lord Jesus Christ."]{.class_s35R}

Ephesians 5:26--27, ["That he might sanctify and cleanse it with the washing of water by the word, That he might present it to himself a glorious church, not having SPOT or wrinkle, or any such thing; but that it should be holy and without blemish."]{.class_s35R}

First Corinthians 1:7--8, ["So that ye come behind in no gift; waiting for the coming of our Lord Jesus Christ: Who shall also confirm you unto the end, that ye may be BLAMELESS in the day of our Lord Jesus Christ."]{.class_s35R}

But what Peter is speaking of here is not a positional thing for the Christian. He is to work at these qualities, so it is a practical thing.

Paul says, ["If it be possible, as much as lieth in you, ]{.class_s35R}[live peaceably with all men]{.class_s35W-0}["]{.class_s35R} (Rom. 12:18). He says in Romans 14:19, ["]{.class_s35R}[Let us therefore follow after the things which make for peace]{.class_s35W-0}[, and things wherewith one may edify another."]{.class_s35R}

In 1 Timothy 6:14, Paul says, ["That thou keep this commandment without spot, unrebukeable, until the appearing of our Lord Jesus Christ."]{.class_s35R}

He says, ["]{.class_s35R}[Do all things without murmurings and disputings]{.class_s35W-0}[: That ye may be blameless and harmless, the sons of God, without rebuke in the midst of a crooked and perverse nation, among whom ye shine as lights in the world"]{.class_s35R} (Phil. 2:14--15). ["And these things give in charge, ]{.class_s35R}[that they may be blameless]{.class_s35W-0}["]{.class_s35R} (1 Tim. 5:7).

So there is a spiritual, practical sense in which a Christian has to [work ]{.class_s35S}at these things to maintain a good testimony before an unsaved world.

But when you hit that ["spot"]{.class_s35R} in the General Epistles, you are no longer in a figurative, spiritual, practical sense. In the Tribulation, that ["spot"]{.class_s35R} is connected with the mark of the beast (Rev. 13:16; 16:2) that is associated with leprosy (Lev. 13--14). In the Tribulation, the believer is ["to keep himself unspotted from the world"]{.class_s35R} (James 1:27) and to hate ["even the garment spotted by the flesh"]{.class_s35R} (Jude 23).

That is why both Peter and Jude wrote so vehemently against the false teachers and prophets, because such people ["are spots in your feasts"]{.class_s35R} (Jude 12; 2 Pet. 2:13). For further study, we recommend you to our Commentaries on James, Jude, and Revelation on the passages above.

Verse 15: ["And account that the longsuffering of our Lord is salvation."]{.class_s35R} That isn't saying that eventually everyone, including the Devil, will be saved ([as Bullinger teaches]{.class_s35S}). It is saying that as long as God is putting up with you, you have a chance to be saved. The problem a sinner has is [presuming ]{.class_s35S}on God's longsuffering. The longer you put off salvation, the closer you come to God cutting off His longsuffering to you. God may give you another [chance to be saved]{.class_s35S}, and then again, [He may not. ]{.class_s35S}You may be like that rich fool in Luke 12:20, and God is ready to cut you off within twenty-four hours.

That is why Paul wrote a word of wisdom (vs. 15) to the sinner in 2 Corinthians 6:2. ["Now is the accepted time; behold, now is the day of salvation."]{.class_s35R} That goes for the practical application that a sinner should get saved [today,]{.class_s35S} and it goes for the doctrinal application that a sinner should get saved during the time when God is offering salvation as a ["free gift"]{.class_s35R} through faith apart from works (Rom. 5; Eph. 2).

A man is a fool if he thinks that he can, or will, get saved in the Tribulation, immediately after the Rapture of the Church. Once that Rapture takes place, the offer of the [free]{.class_s35S} grace of God is gone; you are back under a [faith-and-works]{.class_s35S} setup. Do you really think you will be able to "make it" under a system like that[ when you wouldn't accept salvation as a free gift by faith alone?]{.class_s35S}

Now, 2 Peter 3:15--16 is the Holy Spirit's proof that Pauline epistles are Scripture (vs. 16), and that they are the definitive work on New Testament salvation (vs. 15). Paul speaks of the things about which Peter writes in chapter 3; that is why we have cross referenced his epistles wherever they were applicable. You can't consign Peter's epistle completely to the Tribulation, with no doctrinal application to the Church Age.

"In which are some things hard to be understood, which they that are unlearned and unstable wrest, []{#c307.xhtml_page_481}as they do also the other scriptures, unto their own destruction."

Those are words coming from another apostle of Jesus Christ. Peter had a hard time understanding Paul's teaching on Jews and Gentiles in the Body of Christ and had to be [rebuked by Paul]{.class_s35S} for the mess he made of things in Antioch (Gal. 2:11--14).

Notice the two groups that make a mess of Paul's epistles: the ["unlearned"]{.class_s35R} and the ["unstable."]{.class_s35R} The ["unlearned"]{.class_s35R} are not uneducated. The uneducated can get it (Acts 4:13; 1 Cor. 1:27). A man learns by studying, and the modern Bibles have all removed the [command]{.class_s35S} to study or the [way]{.class_s35S} to study from 2 Timothy 2:15. If Peter had a hard time understanding what Paul taught in Galatians 2, we can forgive him, for at the time Peter had none of Paul's epistles to study. He corrected that problem by the time he got to 2 Peter 3:16.

The ["unstable"]{.class_s35R} are unstable because they haven't grown any in the Lord. They are ["tossed to and fro, and carried about with every wind of doctrine, by the sleight of men"]{.class_s35R} (Eph. 4:13--14).

A Christian is established in the faith when he learns and practises what the Scriptures say (Col. 2:6--7).

When the ["unlearned" ]{.class_s35R}and the ["unstable"]{.class_s35R} handle the Scriptures, they ["wrest"]{.class_s35R} it, i.e., they [twist]{.class_s35S} it, ["unto their own destruction."]{.class_s35R} That Bible is like a ["twoedged sword,"]{.class_s35R} and when you don't know how to handle it, you will cut yourself up spiritually till you are a bloody mess. It's like trying to juggle sixty-six razor blades when you don't know what you are doing.

Now, if you know what Peter says about the Second Coming in chapter 3 and if you know what can happen to a person who twists the Scriptures, then you had better ["beware."]{.class_s35R} You had better watch out whom you follow. You can be ["led away with the error of the wicked."]{.class_s35R}

That's good advice for the Christian. Paul says, ["Beware of dogs, beware of evil workers, beware of the concision"]{.class_s35R} (Phil. 3:2); and the context of that verse is that you are to beware of what they teach about the flesh and self-righteousness. In Colossians 2:8, he says, ["Beware lest any man spoil you through philosophy and vain deceit, after the tradition of men, after the rudiments of the world, and not after Christ."]{.class_s35R}

The ["fall"]{.class_s35R} of verse 17, once again, has nothing to do with falling from or out of [salvation]{.class_s35S}. It is falling ["from your own stedfastness."]{.class_s35R} The ["stedfastness"]{.class_s35R} of the Christian has to do with his service to Christ (1 Cor. 15:58) and his warfare against the world, the flesh, and the Devil (1 Pet. 5:9).

And finally verse 18 takes us right back to chapter 1. Peter wants the disciples whom he has been teaching to ["grow in grace."]{.class_s35R} That was what he described in chapter 1, verses 5--7. And Peter wants them to ["grow\...in the knowledge of our Lord and Saviour Jesus Christ."]{.class_s35R} That growth in grace is connected with that knowledge (2 Pet. 1:2), and when you grow in grace, then you cause your knowledge of Christ to grow and bear fruit (2 Pet. 1:8).

Paul said of this spiritual growth:[ "But speaking the truth in love, may grow up into him in all things, which is the head, even Christ"]{.class_s35R} (Eph. 4:15).

Warning: [no Christian ever grows spiritually who doesn't spend time in the Book,]{.class_s35S} and no Christian will ever get to know his Saviour as he should [who doesn't spend time in the Book!]{.class_s35S}

["To him"]{.class_s35R} (Jesus Christ) ["be glory both now and for ever. Amen."]{.class_s35R}
